proc(point_, p)
local u, v, var, num, den, a, denom_, i;
    var := {x, y};
    num := 2147483564*x*y^49 + 2147483643*x^35*y^8 + 2147483574*y^40
         + 97*x^29*y^9 + 2147483585*y^23;
    denom_ := 1259857073*x^2*y^20 + x^21 + 572662306*x^2*y^19
         + 1832519379*x^2*y^18 + 1947051839*x^10*y^8 + 2090217417*x^9*y^8;
    a := num/denom_;
    return
        Eval(a, {seq(var[i] = point_[i], i = 1 .. numelems(point_))}) mod p
end proc
